    var rsaScriptUrl = 'https://www.blaues-kreuz.de/typo3/sysext/rsaauth/Resources/Public/JavaScript/RsaEncryptionWithLib.min.js';
             function rsaauthInit() {
                 if (typeof TYPO3RsaEncryptionPublicKeyUrl == 'undefined') {
                     console.log("loading rsa stuff");
                     // load rsauth js
                     var script = document.createElement('script');
                     script.src = rsaScriptUrl;
                     script.onload = function () {
                         // make sure RSAEncrypt function exists now and set TYPO3RsaEncryptionPublicKeyUrl
                         if (typeof RSAEncrypt === 'function') {
                             TYPO3RsaEncryptionPublicKeyUrl = '?eID=RsaPublicKeyGenerationController';
                         } else {
                             console.error("There was an error loading RsaEncryptionWithLib, Login will not work.");
                             console.error(rsaScriptUrl + " could not be loaded or does not contain the needed functions.");
                         }
                     };
                     document.head.appendChild(script);
                 }
             }

    <style type="text/css">
     .map {
   height: 800px;
 }
    </style>
    <script type="text/javascript">
     jQuery(function ($) {
 	var results;
 	var map;
 	var geocoder;
 	
 	
 	function tx_ytblaueskreuz_geosearch_initAutocomplete_QuotaAvailable() {
 		if($('#google-settings').data('suggestsenabled')=="0"){
     		//disabled due to 160.000/day average on 20161114
     	}else{
     	
 	    	//Create the autocomplete object, restricting the search to geographical
 	    	// location types.
 	    	autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(
 	    		/** @type {!HTMLInputElement} */(document.getElementById('autocomplete')),
 	    		{types: ['geocode']}
 	    	);
 	    
 	    	// When the user selects an address from the dropdown, populate the address
 	    	// fields in the form.
 	    	autocomplete.addListener('place_changed', function(){
 	    		var place = autocomplete.getPlace();
 	    		
 	    		$("#lat").val(place.geometry.location.lat);
 	    		$("#lng").val(place.geometry.location.lng);
 	    		$("#lastsearch").val($("#autocomplete").val());
 	    		focusGeometry(place.geometry);
 	    		$("#zoom").val(map.getZoom());
 	    	});
 	    }
     	
 	}
 	
 	function focusGeometry(geometry){
 		
 		map.panTo(geometry.location);
 		map.fitBounds(geometry.viewport);
 	}
 	
 	
 	function jumpToTerritory(address){
 		geocoder.geocode( { 'address': address}, function(results, status) {
 			if (status == 'OK') {
 				focusGeometry(results[0].geometry);
 			} else {
 				//alert('Geocode was not successful for the following reason: ' + status);
 			}
 		});
 	}
 	
 	function initAutocomplete() {
     	
 		var service = new google.maps.places.AutocompleteService();
 		try {
 			service.getQueryPredictions({ input: 'wuppertal' }, function(predictions, status){
 				//this will reduce quota by 1 per page view but help auto-detect exceeded quota
 				if (status != google.maps.places.PlacesServiceStatus.OK) {
 				
 				}else{
 					tx_ytblaueskreuz_geosearch_initAutocomplete_QuotaAvailable();
 				}
 			});
 		}catch(error){
 			
 		}
     }
 	
     function showResult(result){
     	result.state = "visible";			
     	result.marker.setMap(map);
     }
     
     function hideResult(result){
     	result.state = "hidden";
     	result.marker.setMap(null);
     }
     
     function updateResults(){
     	var type=$('#einrichtungsTyp').val();
     	
     	if(type=="") visibleResults = results;
     	else {
 	    	var visibleResults = $.grep(results, function (result, i) {
 	            return  jQuery.inArray(type, result.categories) >= 0;
 	        }).slice(0, 999);
     	}
     	
     	$.each(results, function () { if ($.inArray(this, visibleResults) < 0) hideResult(this); });
 		$.each(visibleResults, function () {
 			showResult(this);
 			
 		});
     }
     
     var openPopover = function () {
     	var infoWindow;
 
     	return function (marker) {
 	    	if (infoWindow) infoWindow.close();
 	    	infoWindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow({content: marker.popoverText});
 	    	infoWindow.open(map, marker);
 	    	//map.setCenter(marker.position);
     	}
     } ();
     
 	function initMap() {
 		initAutocomplete();
 		
 		geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
 		
 		var initialLocationDefault = {lat: 51.5167, lng: 9.9167};
 		var initialZoomDefault = 8;
 		
 		if ($("#lat").val() && $("#lng").val()  && $("#zoom").val()) {
 			initialLocationDefault = new google.maps.LatLng($("#lat").val(), $("#lng").val());
 			initialZoomDefault=parseInt($("#zoom").val());
 		}else if (navigator.geolocation) {
 			navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function (position) {
 				initialLocationUser = new google.maps.LatLng(position.coords.latitude, position.coords.longitude);
 				initialZoomDefault=10;
 				initialLocationDefault = initialLocationUser;
 			});
 		}
 		
 		map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('map'), {
 			zoom: initialZoomDefault,
 			center: initialLocationDefault
 		});
 	
 		results = $('#mapResults-data').children().map(function () {
 			var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
 				position: new google.maps.LatLng($(this).data('lat'), $(this).data('lng')),
 				title: $(this).data('name'),
 				icon: $(this).data('image')
 				
 			});
 			marker.addListener('click', function () {
 				openPopover(marker);
 			});
 			marker.popoverText = $(this).html();
 			
 			marker.addListener('click', function () {
 				openPopover(marker);
 			});
 			marker.popoverText = $(this).html();
 			
 			return {
 				name: $(this).data('name'),
 				categories: $(this).data('categories'),
 				marker: marker,
 				state: 'hidden'
 			};
 		}).toArray();
 		
 		$("#einrichtungsTyp").change(function(){
     		updateResults();
     	});
 		
 		$("#bundesland").change(function(){
 			jumpToTerritory($(this).val());
     	});
 		
 		updateResults();
 		
 	}
 
 	window.initMap=initMap;
 	
 	$('<script async defer src="https://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?key='+$('#google-settings').data('apikey')+'&callback=initMap&libraries=places"/>').appendTo('body');
 	
 });
    </script>
